The hotel has a perfect location, being only 5min from the olympic stadium area and the Nanjing eye scenic area. The hotel staff are polite, friendly, and speak perfect english. The hotel rooms, whether city view or river view, are all sublime. Spacious room with spacious bathroom and complimentary drinks in the mini-fridge, the holiday feeling when you enter the room is immediate. The hotel has is home to a number of restaurants that offer a range of meals. Additionally, the hotel buffet is great (cost approx 350CNY) and includes a variety of meal options from seafood to steak to vegetarian options. I stay at this hotel once or twice per year and i thoroughly enjoy the stay each time.

name:J‚Äço‚Äçs‚Äçh‚ÄçS‚ÄçW‚ÄçT
info:Luxury Room - River-View (Double Bed)
info:Stayed in July 2022
info:Couples
info:1 Review
rating:4.2
posted:Posted July 21, 2022
msg:---------- Good things ----------
The service is good and the breakfast is well catered, the staff work hard to fulfill the needs of guests. 
The room is clean. Bed is changed twice per day, if you don't need a service they will acknowledge that. 
No smoking policy is strictly enforced, so the hotel has a very pleasant smell. 
Air conditioning in the room is superior to that of competitor hotels, it actually cools the whole room.
The minibar is stocked with complimentary (free) products upon arrival, coconut water can, herbal tea can, sprite can and orange juice small bottle.
Fruits are provided on arrival.
Swimming pool is free, gym is free, sauna is free, steam room is free.
Beautiful views.
Buffet dinner is expensive but overall worth it, unlimited drinks, a good variety of food, western and Chinese food.
The walls are thick, very quiet rooms, and you can play music and it's difficult for people outside to hear.

----------- Bad things -----------
Visiting the swimming pool, my towel was on the side of the pool, and it was taken away without notice, asked where to get a towel from staff member, the staff said "I don't know" and walked away.
Fridge didn't work initially so needed replacing. 
Reading light switches are incorrectly wired.
Some dirt on the switches.
International calling is not free.
I had late night, and put on do not disturb so I wouldn't get disturbed whilst I was sleeping during the daytime, we received a phone call to ask if this was really the case and if room service was required. (Maybe this isn't bad for most people, I appreciate the care, but it did wake me up).
Changing rooms close at 10pm, but gym is 24 hours, so make sure to get changed in your room.



Extra notes, please be sure to read before booking:

----- In the picture there is a red light, in the bathroom mirror, do not be afraid, it's not a camera, the mirror has a TV, which was a massive relief. -----
Swimming caps are required for the pool, you can use the free shower caps, but they sell swimming caps for 90CNY.
A good selection of restaurants and bars nearby if you don't want the hotel food.
Shavers are free but need to ask for them.
Shampoo, conditioner and body wash provided but in small bottles.
Afternoon tea has a price of around 300 to 400CNY.

It is worth the price, however as with any hotel there's room for improvement, I would personally recommend a stay here.

The gym is 24 hours, with water and towels, and there is also a swimming pool (open until 10 o'clock).
After dinner and returning to the room, I found that the hotel seemed to have helped me with the night bed service.
Great, the hotel was recommended by a friend, and I will also recommend this hotel to other friends

msg:Let me talk about the overall evaluation first: As a luxury hotel that has been in business for 5 years and advertises itself as a "seven-star" hotel, the price of the river view room after the epidemic has exceeded 1,500, and its hardware facilities, service awareness, and service methods cannot match. The location of the hotel is superior, and the river view is excellent, but its software and hardware, especially its service methods and service awareness, all reveal a kind of arrogance that matches the city of Nanjing, a kind of arrogance unique to the old and young, and the children of officials in the system.

At any moment, the arrogance revealed by the service industry is tantamount to a dislocation of the platform as its own ability, an illusory sense of ownership, which is ridiculous and sad.

Facilities: The size of the room is good, but the bedding is not satisfactory. The pillows are only equipped with feather soft pillows by default, and there is no default soft/hard pillow option. It really affects sleep in the middle of the night. After ITU, buckwheat pillows are sent, and there is no high latex pillow option;

In terms of facilities, what is ridiculous is the TV in the room, which looks like a 40-inch (maybe less than) low-definition TV in the style of an old state-owned hotel in the 1990s, which is jaw-dropping. What is even more ridiculous than the TV is that it is not equipped with a TV remote control (only the smart system remote control), so that the volume of the smart system is turned up to the maximum, and the TV still has very limited sound.

I called the service staff and finally brought the TV remote control. Then I found that there was no battery. After a lot of trouble, I finally turned up the volume and asked: Why don‚Äôt you put the TV remote control directly in the room and put it away separately?

Answer: Is the volume satisfactory now?

Ask again: It's not the volume problem. Is there any reason why the remote control of the most basic hotel facility like TV doesn't appear in the room?

He replied again: Is the volume satisfactory now?

...

After being speechless for a while, the waiter finally replied: Because most of the guests don't know how to use the two remote controls where they are placed, so there is no need to give them.

Astonished, the waiter pulled out the battery again, put it into another electrical appliance, and walked away.

Thanks to the service staff for giving us a moment of freedom to use the TV remote.


Service: Still like Nanjing, a city of state-owned enterprises, the hotel has to go through three sets of waiters (security guard, concierge, front desk) and two elevators from the first floor to the guest rooms, and as they said, they belong to different depar**ents. With so many redundant staff and such complicated depar**ent settings, people can fully understand what it means to be a state-owned enterprise, what it means to sweep the snow before each person, and what it means for three monks to have no water to eat.

In the middle of the night, I suddenly had a fever, so I ordered two takeaways, one was emergency medicine, and the other was stomach-warming wontons.

Thanks to my brother's repeated instructions, the medicine was finally delivered to the hotel room 15 minutes after it was delivered.

Wonton became more and more twists and turns, maybe it was night, and the security guards downstairs became extremely irritable, as if it was impossible for guests staying in this seven-star hotel to have a meal in the middle of the night.

According to the delivery boy‚Äôs feedback, the security guard provided him with the food delivery process: put it in the takeaway cabinet first, or the customer can go to the first floor to pick up the food from the 50th or 60th floor, or call the hotel front desk to check and ask the hotel front desk to send someone to pick it up.

According to the feedback from the front desk: they are willing to pick it up, but first the guests have to call to inform them of the specific meal pick-up code to check whether it is their own meal.

Angrily said: Why do you want customers to pay for the redundancy and confusion of your hotel's internal depar**ent settings?

He also said: Even if it is a small matter that can be done by a random express hotel, a note, and a food delivery robot today in 2023, it will be done through three groups of employees, three depar**ents, plus repeated phone calls from the customer himself and the delivery boy. Is this showing dignity or stupidity?

Answer: We send people, we send people.


To sum up, as a 30-year-old Nanjing, I already know the tonality of this city well. I chose Jumeirah because I wanted to have a comfortable and peaceful staycation. No one wants to experience again and again what is buck-passing, what is light-speed dumping, what is superfluous, and what is the disadvantage of the system during such a comfortable journey.

These, we have endured enough in our daily life, appearing in such a hotel, such a itinerary, I cannot accept it. This kind of service awareness and service method, such "official standard" (even hard to call it an official) magic realism that does not take the convenience of the guests, appears in any luxury hotel, which is like a farce.

Ridiculous, but annoying.
